She proved to us that you can be filled with skills, and it definitely shows in her artwork. These pixel 3D illustrations are just hit right in the spot, and they are nostalgic too. Most of the electronics from that era are dated but were very appreciated and most loved by our generation but also to the generation to come. Here some more of her work and you'll get lose yourself in it, inspired by all the little details and angles of her illustration. class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Since the coronavirus pandemic, there has been a heightened interest in getting the NYT paper delivered. This campaign aims to address this new need — <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/ZwarteKoffie\">Timo Kuilder</a> and team convince readers to upgrade to a higher frequency of delivery by staying connected and informed at their own pace and get in-depth understanding of the news during uncertain times.</p>\n\n<p>They made 10 moving illustrations which depict reading the NYT newspaper as part of one's daily home routines.</p>\n\n<h3>Sketches</h3>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"corona delivery New York Times newspaper nyt pandemic paper\" class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/reinventing-graphic-design-handbook-\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/09cda5122205899.60d4b1817d7b3.jpeg\" width=\"1400\" height=\"1072\" alt=\"Reinventing the 'graphic design' handbook\" title=\"Reinventing the 'graphic design' handbook\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>07.09.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>We are taking a look at <a href=\"https://theguide.design/\">theguide.design</a> which is a platform designed for 'Shillington Graphic Design course'. An experience designed by the fine folks from <a href=\"https://standingby.company/\">Standing By Co.</a> where they have built an ultimate digital guide to learn the basics of graphic design. What a great way to reinvent the digital experience of a handbook, I hope the students will enjoy this unique experience. Through the overall experience and the transitions; what I think I love the most about the experience is how adaptable it is. What I would implement if it was my experience, I would probably have a mobile version to fill those late-night reading use cases!</p>\n\n<ul><li>See the full case study on : <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/gallery/122205899/The-Guide\">Behance</a></li>\n</ul><blockquote>The Guide is an online platform that showcases supporting material for the Shillington Graphic Design course. The Guide has over 20 years of content created by hundreds of teachers globally.</blockquote>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/383170748\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1440px;margin:auto;\"><!-- You're using demo endpoint of Iframely API commercially. class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/designer-spotlight-guillaume-azadian-\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/Reuters-case-study_12.jpg\" width=\"2560\" height=\"1999\" alt=\"Designer Spotlight — Guillaume Azadian\" title=\"Designer Spotlight — Guillaume Azadian\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>07.08.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>It's been a little while since our last 'Spotlight' series and it's always rewarding to feature designers, leaders who are excelling in what they do but usually are just part of the behind-the-scenes of a major brand overhaul or product releases. It's great to share their work and learn more about their background, passion, and more. Let me share the work of <a href=\"http://www.guillaumeazadian.com/\">Guillaume Azadian</a>, a designer and an interactive design director based in Paris, France. He has been in the field for more than 10 years and had the opportunity to work with really well-established brands. For the feature, I decided to feature two case studies, one for designing the world's biggest shop window for news with '<a href=\"http://www.guillaumeazadian.com/work/reuters-connect/\">Reuters Connect Platform</a>' and the other on rethinking the digital experience for '<a href=\"http://www.guillaumeazadian.com/work/harvard-business-executive-education/\">Harvard Business School</a>'. For more of Guillaume's work, make sure to check out this site below.</p>\n\n<ul><li>More on Guillaume Azadian : <a href=\"http://www.guillaumeazadian.com/\">guillaumeazadian.com</a></li>\n</ul><blockquote>I've had the pleasure to work with clients such as Reuters, Harvard Business School, Marriott, Google, Formula Design\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/african-bloom-holdings-brand-identity-presentation-design\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_african_bloom.jpg\" width=\"1504\" height=\"1281\" alt=\"African Bloom Holdings - Brand Identity & Presentation Design\" title=\"African Bloom Holdings - Brand Identity & Presentation Design\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>07.12.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/simaclennan\">Si Maclennan</a> shared a branding, visual identity and presentation design for African Bloom Holdings, a consumer goods company in the cannabis product market. African Bloom manages a diverse brand platform, and creates value by giving consumers access to best-in-class products, designed to satisfy key segments within the medical, wellness, and recreational markets. The company needed a corporate identity and various elements to support fundraising efforts.</p>\n\n<p>The African Bloom logo is inspired by the Strelitzia, or \"Bird of Paradise\" flower - a species of flora endemic to South Africa, and a national symbol of the region. The flower was chosen as a way to bring naturally inspired shapes into the logo without turning to cannabis leaves that are ubiquitous in the industry. The flower is rendered in a minimalist geometric style that gives it a distinctly African feeling, while retaining a modern look.</p>\n\n<p> </p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"african src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/image_processing20210628-11706-f5kvbn.jpeg\" width=\"1600\" height=\"1200\" alt=\"Dribbble Spotlight — Illustrations by Isaac LeFever \" title=\"Dribbble Spotlight — Illustrations by Isaac LeFever \" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>07.08.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>It's been quite a while since I last spent time looking for inspiration on <a href=\"https://dribbble.com/\">Dribbble</a>. Not to brag but things are most or less the same which is unfortunate, to be honest. But on the good side, I stumbled across the work of <a href=\"http://shop.nicetriangle.com/\">Isaac LeFever</a>, which by the way is a badass name to start with. Isaac is an art director & illustrator based in Seattle, WA, USA. After browsing through his work, I have a huge fan of the overall visual style. It somehow reminds me of the encyclopedias I used to read when I was younger where the colors were always warm, the print quality was textured with a pattern, and somehow always yellow-ish. These pieces are sublime and stunning, I took the liberty to share a few below, make sure to follow his work on <a href=\"https://dribbble.com/nicetriangle/\">Dribbble</a>.</p>\n\n<ul><li>More on Photo Manipulations\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>07.07.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Let's be clear. I really don't miss the days of home quarantine from the past year. I did appreciate the time spent with the loved ones but glad we all get to live some kind of a 'normal' summertime. With that being said, it's always rewarding to see how others had to cope with this pandemic and what needed to be done to actually stay sane. I really love this series by <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/martindepasquale\">Martín De Pasquale</a> titled: 'Surreal portraits 2020-2021' where it's basically a series of experiments during his home quarantine. And they are so incredible, it totally reminds me of the days of photo manipulations performed in Photoshop that would either twist your mind or spam your creativity. You really should check out the full project on <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/martindepasquale/\">Behance</a>, Martín took the liberty to include a few short clips as well. It's a delight!</p>\n\n<ul><li>More on Martín De Pasquale : <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/martindepasquale/\">behance.net/martindepasquale</a></li>\n</ul><blockquote>A selection of work performed 02:35:48","updatedTime":"2021-07-13 02:35:48","title":"Hermes Mazali’s take at 36 Days of Type","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/rv9T537GFvU/hermes-mazalis-take-36-days-type","description":"Hermes Mazali’s take at 36 Days of Type\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/hermes-mazalis-take-36-days-type\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/03441097172617.5ebed087bd7b1.gif\" width=\"1080\" height=\"1080\" alt=\"Hermes Mazali’s take at 36 Days of Type\" title=\"Hermes Mazali’s take at 36 Days of Type\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>07.11.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"http://hmazali.com/\">Hermes Mazali</a> has shared his take of the series <a href=\"http://www.36daysoftype.com/\">36 Days of Type</a> and thought it would totally deserve its own feature on abdz. You know how much we are personally fans of this initiative and it's always inspiring, intriguing, and exciting to see how much people are talented and proud to share their work. Hermes went all out with a set of language that shares a common contrast combination of colors, probably to replicate and support its concept. To me, I feel there is some kind of 'cyberpunk-esque' feel to it, especially it's time to be creative with the types. Make sure to check out <a href=\"http://hmazali.com/\">Hermes's personal site</a> and beyond.</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"http://hmazali.com\">http://hmazali.com</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/Hmazali\">https://www.behance.net/Hmazali</a></li>\n</ul><blockquote>... for a long time I needed to reconnect with my profession and that's why I chose this project. I enjoyed the process and met a lot of creatives around the world, I even had the pleasure of having a feature by the curators of the project!</blockquote>\n\n<p><img href=\"https://www.behance.net/mariaboada\">Maria Boada</a> are respectively brand designer and illustrator based in Lima, Peru. They have worked together to design this grand brand identity & packaging for Yaro Sushi Experience which is also based in Peru. I think what caught my eye is the use of the red color mixed with the beige and let's not forget about the gold foil which brings a premium finish to the overall packaging. On the last note, props to Daniela for the fantastic photography and presentation as well.
